\newcommand{\hide}[2]{
\ifthenelse{\equal{#1}{inherited}}%
{}%
{}%
}
\newcommand{\entityintro}[3]{%
  \hbox to \hsize{%
    \vbox{%
      \hbox to .2in{}%
    }%
    {\bf #1}%
    \dotfill\pageref{#2}%
  }
  \makebox[\hsize]{%
    \parbox{.4in}{}%
    \parbox[l]{5in}{%
      \vspace{1mm}\it%
      #3%
      \vspace{1mm}%
    }%
  }%
}
\newcommand{\isep}[0]{%
\setlength{\itemsep}{-.4ex}
}
\newcommand{\sld}[0]{%
%\setlength{\topsep}{0em}
%\setlength{\partopsep}{0em}
%\setlength{\parskip}{0em}
%\setlength{\parsep}{-1em}
}
\newcommand{\headref}[3]{%
\ifthenelse{#1 = 1}{%
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{\hspace{\qquad}\protect\numberline{}{#3}}%
}{}%
\ifthenelse{#1 = 2}{%
\addcontentsline{toc}{subsection}{\hspace{\qquad}\protect\numerline{}{#3}}%
}{}%
\ifthenelse{#1 = 3}{%
\addcontentsline{toc}{subsubsection}{\hspace{\qquad}\protect\numerline{}{#3}}%
}{}%
\label{#3}%
\makebox[\textwidth][l]{#2 #3}%
}%
\newcommand{\membername}[1]{{\it #1}\linebreak}
\newcommand{\divideents}[1]{\vskip -1em\indent\rule{2in}{.5mm}}
\newcommand{\refdefined}[1]{
\expandafter\ifx\csname r@#1\endcsname\relax
\relax\else
{$($ in \ref{#1}, page \pageref{#1}$)$}
\fi}
\newcommand{\startsection}[4]{
\gdef\classname{#2}
\subsection{\label{#3}{\bf {\sc #1} #2}}{
\rule[1em]{\hsize}{4pt}\vskip -1em
\vskip .1in 
#4
}%
}
\newcommand{\startsubsubsection}[2]{
\subsubsection{\sc #1}{%
\rule[1em]{\hsize}{2pt}%
#2}
}

 of our game.}

 of our game.}

\startsection{Class}{DifficultyAction}{l1}{%
{\small Takes care of showing a New Game-dialog to the user
 and start a new game based on their difficultychoice.}
\vskip .1in 
\startsubsubsection{Declaration}{
\fbox{\vbox{
\hbox{\vbox{\small public 
class 
DifficultyAction}}
\noindent\hbox{\vbox{{\bf extends} javax.swing.AbstractAction}}
}}}
\startsubsubsection{Serializable Fields}{
\begin{itemize}
\item{
private MainInterface component\begin{itemize}\item{\vskip -.9ex }\end{itemize}
}
\end{itemize}
}
\startsubsubsection{Constructors}{
\vskip -2em
\begin{itemize}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{DifficultyAction}
{\tt public {\bf DifficultyAction}( {\tt view.MainInterface } {\bf component},
{\tt model.Game } {\bf game},
{\tt java.lang.Boolean } {\bf firstScreen} )
\label{l25}\label{l26}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Creates a DifficultyAction associated with the component and
 based on the game.
 
 The firstScreen-flag determines if there should be an
 "Are you sure?"-dialog before showing the difficultyselection.
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt component} - The MainInterface to associate the action with}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt game} - The game to reset if the user wants to start a new game}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt firstScreen} - Enables the "Are you sure"-dialog if firstScreen is false}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}
\startsubsubsection{Methods}{
\vskip -2em
\begin{itemize}

\membername{actionPerformed}
{\tt public void {\bf actionPerformed}( {\tt java.awt.event.ActionEvent } {\bf e} )
\label{l27}\label{l28}}%end signature
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}

\newpage
\def\packagename{view}
\chapter{\bf Package view}{
\vskip -.25in
\hbox to \hsize{\it Package Contents\hfil Page}
\rule{\hsize}{.7mm}
\vskip .13in
\hbox{\bf Interfaces}
\entityintro{MainInterface}{l55}{Interface for the two different kinds of windows our
 program containts.}
\vskip .13in
\hbox{\bf Classes}
\entityintro{Background}{l56}{Handles the drawing of the backgroundimage.}
\entityintro{Board}{l57}{The graphical representation of our Sudokuboard.}
\entityintro{CongratulationScreen}{l58}{A congratulationscreen used to congratulate the user
 when they have completed a Sudokupuzzle.}
\entityintro{DifficultySelection}{l59}{A screen used to let the user select between
 the different difficulties.}
\entityintro{Header}{l60}{The headerimage (the "title").}
\entityintro{IngameControls}{l61}{The ingamecontrols (Help- and New Game-button)}
\entityintro{MainApplet}{l62}{Our program in Applet-form.}
\entityintro{MainWindow}{l63}{...no description...}
\entityintro{NumberDialog}{l64}{...no description...}
\entityintro{PlaceCenter}{l65}{Class containg a function to center a component.}
\entityintro{SheepSpeak}{l66}{The SheepSpeak, which is our main method to
 communicate with the users.}
\entityintro{Statistics}{l67}{...no description...}
\entityintro{SudokuButton}{l68}{Creates buttons based on images.}
\entityintro{SudokuMenu}{l69}{A menubar containing the proper menuitems.}
\entityintro{ViewSettings}{l70}{Abstract class containing the various settings
 used in the GUI.}
\vskip .1in
\rule{\hsize}{.7mm}
\vskip .1in
\newpage

\sld

\label{l150}\label{l151}}%end signature

   \item{

\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt frame} - The frame the screen should be added to.}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt difficultyAction} - The DifficultyAction showing the New Game-screen.}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt helpAction} - The HelpAction handling requests for help.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}

\newpage
\def\packagename{model}
\chapter{\bf Package model}{
\vskip -.25in
\hbox to \hsize{\it Package Contents\hfil Page}
\rule{\hsize}{.7mm}
\vskip .13in
\hbox{\bf Interfaces}
\entityintro{GameSettings}{l280}{Interface to retrieve GameSettings}
\vskip .13in
\hbox{\bf Classes}
\entityintro{Board}{l281}{Board.java is able to generate sudoku boards, get values from  
 fields and set values in fields.}
\entityintro{EasySettings}{l282}{The easy gamesettings for a 9x9 Sudoku.}
\entityintro{Game}{l283}{Contains the gameboard and the solution.}
\entityintro{General9x9Settings}{l284}{Contains the general settings for a 9x9 sudoku}
\entityintro{Generator}{l285}{The sudoku generator.}
\entityintro{HardSettings}{l286}{The hard gamesettings for a 9x9 Sudoku.}
\entityintro{Helper}{l287}{Helper.java is able to find a field thats solveable, find fields that are
 incorrectly filled in and how many mistakes present on the board.}
\entityintro{NormalSettings}{l288}{The normal gamesettings for a 9x9 Sudoku.}
\entityintro{Solver}{l289}{Solver class used to solve a Sudoku-puzzle.}
\entityintro{Statistics}{l290}{The statistics of the current game.}
\entityintro{SudokuMath}{l291}{Performs various mathematical operations on SudokuBoards.}
\vskip .1in
\rule{\hsize}{.7mm}
\vskip .1in
\newpage

\section{Classes}{
\startsection{Class}{Board}{l281}{%
{\small Board.java is able to generate sudoku boards, get values from  
 fields and set values in fields.
 It can compare two boards to check if the sudoku is solved.}
\vskip .1in 
\startsubsubsection{Declaration}{
\fbox{\vbox{
\hbox{\vbox{\small public 
class

\noindent\hbox{\vbox{{\bf extends} java.util.Observable}}
}}}

\startsection{Class}{Game}{l283}{%
{\small Contains the gameboard and the solution.
 When a new game is created Game will create a new board.}
\vskip .1in 
\startsubsubsection{Declaration}{
\fbox{\vbox{
\hbox{\vbox{\small public 
class 
Game}}
\noindent\hbox{\vbox{{\bf extends} java.lang.Object}}
}}}
\startsubsubsection{Constructors}{
\vskip -2em
\begin{itemize}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{Game}
{\tt public {\bf Game}(  )
\label{l346}\label{l347}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Stores the solved board in solutionBoard. Makes the generator
 remove numbers until the desired difficulty is reached and then 
 stores the new board in currentBoard
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}

{\tt model.Board } {\bf board} )
\label{l404}\label{l405}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{

 unable to produce a unique result, call solverLevelTwo.
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}

\sld

\sld

  \end{itemize}

the result of trying to solve the field, 0 if not solveable. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}

\startsection{Class}{SudokuMath}{l291}{%
{\small Performs various mathematical operations on SudokuBoards.
 Everything is 0-index'ed, and works on boards of all sizes. 
 Fx. a row from a 3x3x9 Sudoku has the numbers 0 to 8.}
\vskip .1in 
\startsubsubsection{Declaration}{
\fbox{\vbox{
\hbox{\vbox{\small public abstract 
class 
SudokuMath}}
\noindent\hbox{\vbox{{\bf extends} java.lang.Object}}
}}}
\startsubsubsection{Constructors}{
\vskip -2em
\begin{itemize}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{SudokuMath}
{\tt public {\bf SudokuMath}(  )
\label{l420}\label{l421}}%end signature
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}
\startsubsubsection{Methods}{
\vskip -2em
\begin{itemize}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getColumnFromPos}
{\tt public static int {\bf getColumnFromPos}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.Board } {\bf board} )
\label{l422}\label{l423}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Gets the contents of the column based on the position in the board.
 This is done by first calculating the columnNumber, 
 adding the value this position contains to an array, 
 and then continuously adding boardDim to the columnNumber, 
 adding that value to the array until the array has boardDimension 
 values in it.
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position to get the column from.}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt board} - The board to get the column from.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
An int-array containing the column. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\divideents{getColumnNumber}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getColumnNumber}
{\tt public static int {\bf getColumnNumber}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.GameSettings } {\bf settings} )
\label{l424}\label{l425}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Converts a position to a columnnumber, 
 by calculating (position \% boardDimension).
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position on the board.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
The number of the column. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\divideents{getQuadrantFromPos}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getQuadrantFromPos}
{\tt public static int {\bf getQuadrantFromPos}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.Board } {\bf board} )
\label{l426}\label{l427}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Gets the contents of the quadrant based on the position in the board.
 It calculates the fieldId of the top left corner of the quadrant, and 
 then adds the fieldIds based on the size of the board.
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position to get the quadrant from.}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt board} - The board to get the cquadrant from.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
An int-array containing the quadrant. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\divideents{getQuadrantNumber}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getQuadrantNumber}
{\tt public static int {\bf getQuadrantNumber}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.GameSettings } {\bf settings} )
\label{l428}\label{l429}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Converts a position to a quadrantnumber, by calculating
 ((rowNumber $/$ quadrantDim) * quadrantDim + columnNumber $/$ quadrantDim).
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position on the board.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
The number of the quadrant. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\divideents{getRowFromPos}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getRowFromPos}
{\tt public static int {\bf getRowFromPos}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.Board } {\bf board} )
\label{l430}\label{l431}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Gets the contents of the row based on the position in the board.
 This is done by substracting the columnNumber from the position value,
 and adding values to an int-array until it has reached the length
 of the boardDimension.
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position to get the row from.}
   \item{
\sld
{\tt board} - The board to get the row from.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
An int-array containing the row. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\divideents{getRowNumber}
\item{\vskip -1.9ex 
\membername{getRowNumber}
{\tt public static int {\bf getRowNumber}( {\tt int } {\bf position},
{\tt model.GameSettings } {\bf settings} )
\label{l432}\label{l433}}%end signature
\begin{itemize}
\sld
\item{
\sld
{\bf Usage}
  \begin{itemize}\isep
   \item{
Converts a position to a rownumber, 
 by calculating (position $/$ boardDimension).
}%end item
  \end{itemize}
}
\item{
\sld
{\bf Parameters}
\sld\isep
  \begin{itemize}
\sld\isep
   \item{
\sld
{\tt position} - The position on the board.}
  \end{itemize}
}%end item
\item{{\bf Returns} - 
The number of the row. 
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}%end item
\end{itemize}
}
}
}
}

\sld
{\bf Usage}

   \item{

 fieldId is returned, plus no Exception is thrown.
